msg:Yangshuo is one of those places I hold close to me heart. The landscape is just so unique and so beautiful. 

So for my third trip to Yangshuo, I thought I would try a new location to stay. I came across this hotel on the mountain top and decided to give it a go. 

Now, due to the location being on top one of the mountains, it did mean driving through some winding mountain roads to get there. But it was well worth it. The view is spectacular!!! 

My room was clean and spacious, and the restaurant had a nice selection for breakfast, afternoon tea and dinner. But what shone through was the service. 

I was assigned to butler XiaoZhen who gave me a link so I could contact her at anytime during my stay if I had any questions. Her service was more than I could ask for. From reminding me when the restaurant was opened, to giving me advice for my itinerary during my stay, she went over and beyond to ensure my stay was pleasant.
